21/10/2022, 12:05â€¯pm - +234 803 433 4350: UNILORIN Final Year, PG students resume Oct. 24
*Others resume Dec 15

Following the suspension of the prolonged strike by the Academic Staff Union of Universities  (ASUU), the University of Ilorin has concluded arrangements for the resumption of academic activities  on Monday, October 24, 2022.

This follows the ratification of the  amended Academic Calendar  by the University Senate at its 291st meeting on Friday, October 21, 2022.

According to the amended Calendar, Final Year and Postgraduate students are expected back on campus on Monday, 24th October, 2022, while other categories of returning students will resume on December 15th when the 2021/2022 academic session commences.

Also, students of the Faculties of Agriculture and Veterinary Medicine, who are yet to complete their Rain Semestre examinations before the commencement of the strike on February 14, 2022, are expected to resume on October 24th to conclude such examinations.

Signed 
Kunle Akogun,
Director of Corporate Affairs, UNILORIN
21st October, 2022

*STUDENTS' UNION*
KADUNA NZEOGWU BUILDING
UNIVERSITY OF ILORIN
_2020/2021 ACADEMIC SESSION_

*PRESS RELEASE*

21/10/2022
12:46PM

*UPDATE ON RESUMPTION DATE*

This is to inform you that the management has fixed *Monday 24th October, 2022* as resumption date for final year students of the University for the completion of the 2020/2021 Academic Session. Subsequently, other returning and fresh students are to resume for a new session on *15th December, 2022*.

The students should also note that final year clearance is expected to commence across various units and departments immediately.

Consequently, private and public hostels will be opened on Monday 24th October, 2022 to accommodate final year students, students of faculties of Veterinary Medicine and Agriculture students who are yet to complete their exams before the commencement of the strike and also faculty of education students on teaching practice or peer teaching program.

The hostel is being opened on Monday to enable cleaning and fumigation to safeguard the lives of our colleagues. 

We hope to see you soon.

#PeopleFocused
 
 Signed:
 TAOFIK, Waliu Opeyemi
 *OMOLUABI*
 _Executive President_
 
 Signed:
 OLABODE, Stephen Opeyemi
 *O' SMART*
 _Public Relations Officer_

09/11/2022, 9:16â€¯pm - +234 803 433 4350: *No free cents in America*

By

_K. O. Babalola_

One book introduction I read as a junior school boy, which has remained permanently in my memory, is the introduction to D. O. Fagunwa's "Ogboju Ode ninu Igbo Irunmole". He said (my translation):

"One beautiful afternoon, I sat in the frontage of my house enjoying the cool breeze of the noon when an old man appeared. He sought permission to sit with me and said he would like to tell the story of his life so that it doesn't die with him."

The above introduction may aptly fit for the short story of Baba Dr P. F. Olaolu. Though he didn't request he wanted it written so it won't die with him, but the japa trend of this age has compelled me to assume the role of Fagunwa in writing down Baba's story as he said it to me. Perhaps, the story may live after as he has passed on.

I finished in Obafemi Awolowo University in 1994 with the best result in my Department and Faculty and one of the top ten in the University. It was a first class in Mathematics, the fourth since its establishment in 1962. For that feat, I was given automatic employment as a graduate assistant, which I took up after youth service in May 1995.

The news of the great feat got to Baba Olaolu - an elder townsman - and he invited me for a honour's get-together. Present at the get-together were five of us: Baba mi, Buoda mi, Baba Yinka, Baba Olaolu himself and myself. It was a beautiful late morning. The day was bright. Baba had arranged a few wooden chairs and a long bench for our arrival. We took our seat and enjoyed the late morning breeze as we were served coconut slices, groundnuts and cups of water.

As we sat at the frontage of the small house, which could pass for a below-average salary earner's house, my eyes took a quick tour of the house as far as they could and there were no sights of attraction. The house betrayed the status of even an ordinary diaspora returnee, much less a full-career surgeon! Baba Olaolu had spent his full medical career life in diaspora. He had just returned home after retirement around the time I graduated.

Baba Olaolu sat with us on a wooden chair. He said to me:

"Omo mi, what is that you are seeing?"

He pointed to the ground. I didn't see anything that I could suspect he meant. So, I answered him in disaffirmation: nothing, sir.

"Is it not sand you are seeing on the ground?"

I said: yes, sir.

*"This is the sand you find anywhere in world. There is no place where currencies lay on the face of the earth for pick. So, if you need anything to take outside the country, please take it and return home to pursue your career. I see you having opportunities but don't be deceived by them. There is no place like home. I have been to places so many that if I tell you that the countries I have visited are more than I did not, I may not be exaggerating! I once worked as a consultant on crew to Radio Germany and they took me places all over the world. Here, I am.... This is what I wish to advise you. Keep it."*

We thanked Baba. We rose and departed.

Since 1995, I have kept Baba's words in front of me guaging my moves with them. Baba did not remember to say:

"I don't want my story to die with me."

He passed on years later. Before his death, he had resorted to farming in the village: not as a passion or pastime but for want of sustenance. Baba was well over eighty at death. In spite of his education and his revered medical profession, he had to  resort to farming in the twilight of his life just to make ends meet. Incredible! You may be asking why he didn't go into private medical practice. He wanted it and he actually tried, but he just couldn't afford such facilities he was used to in diaspora and he was such a principled person who would not dare kill a fly by accident.

That is Baba's story. In it are lessons to learn for the discerning mind. Baba lived his useful working life abroad and now he was back home advising against it! By any reasonable evaluation, the words he possibly held back from saying were that he has gravely regretted his (mis)adventure.

In December 2016, I was in Banjul for a conference with my boss - a Professor of Orthorhinolaryngology (Ear, Nose and Throat, ENT) - and I quizzed him: Oga, is it likely that a Consultant Surgeon in Nigeria would ended up farming later in life for want of food? Being a Muslim, he said: "Olohun o ni je ki a ri aburu." That is, except by the will of Allah, may Allah protect us, it is most unlikely.

Even as Baba did not request me to write his story, I owe him a duty to, most especially now, in this age and time that the wind of a madness called japa is blowing fast.

In Baba's words again:

"There is no place where currencies lay on the face of the earth for pick ... and there is no place like home."

O japarian! There are no free cents on the ground in America.

My one kobo advice.

_Babalola is a Professor of  Mathematical Analysis at the University of Ilorin._

21/11/2022
06:17PM

*NOTICE TO GRADUATING STUDENTS*

The feature for Final Year Student Passport Upload which was earlier removed has been re-enabled. Concerned students should proceed to the portal to upload their passport and check their certificate name format and spelling.

To confirm your certificate name, click "Final Year Student Passport Upload" option on the left sidebar of your undergraduate portal. There, you will see how your name will be arranged on your certificate.

The certificate name should be in the format below:

(First Name) - (Middle Name) - (Last Name/Surname)

It is *COMPULSORY* that *ALL GRADUATING STUDENTS* upload their passports on or before *WEDNESDAY 23RD NOVEMBER, 2022.*

06/12/2022, 5:37â€¯pm - BoluğŸ‘©â€âš–ï¸: Slide 1

Scholarships come in various forms. We have partial, full, studentship, Teaching Assistant, Research Assistant, andÂ  Tuition waiver et al. Also, scholarships from Universities, Governments, Organizations, and Individuals.

There is no clear compartmentalization between some of the scholarships, as some of them are interwoven.

Scholarships are often targeted at indigents/ academic achievers/ those that are helping their community.Â  Some scholarships can combine any of the three or standalone.

PS: Scholarship is not for only First class graduate. if you have a 2.2. you can win prestigious scholarships.
06/12/2022, 5:37â€¯pm - BoluğŸ‘©â€âš–ï¸: Slide 2

Getting scholarships is all about information; if you are not informed you'd be deformed. There are a thousand and one great scholarship opportunities around the world, but most of us don't know about them. You can get scholarships information from blogs, sites, school webs, et al. You need to plan ahead about the scholarships you'd like to apply for. Know the key dates (application start date and deadline) and the requirements; with these, you'd be able to have a workable plan. You can create an excel file to input list of scholarships you will like to apply for and their opening and closing date. This will help you keep track of every scholarship.
06/12/2022, 5:37â€¯pm - BoluğŸ‘©â€âš–ï¸: Slide 3

Before you apply to any scholarship, ask yourself, these three questions.
â–ª Is the scholarship genuine? (There are many scammers who aim to exploit scholars) So it is your 
responsibility to find out if it is a scam or not
â–ª Am I eligible?
â–ª What are my chances?
As soon as you answer these questions, then, proceed to gather documents needed to secure a scholarship

Documents Required 
The documents required for scholarship application process include:

- Transcript/ statement of results 
- Proof of English test (IELTS, TOEFL, GRE or medium of instruction letter from your uni attestating that English is used as a medium of instruction during your study). In UK, some university accept a 
credit pass in your WAEC in lieu of other proof of English. I used my WAEC.

NB: IELTS is British oriented while TOEFL is US oriented but GRE is not English proficiency test. it is usually taken by people in STEM field for admissions and scholarships usually in the US. It's also optional for some schools in the US. You can get scholarship without writing any of these tests. 
It is all about information. I'd advise you to take the exam(s) *if required*, as it won't limit your applications. Also, don't rush to take any of the exams.

- Certificate ,if available (or notification of result) 
- Curriculum Vitae (CV)- Preferbaly academic CV.
- Published literature(s) (journals) (sometimes optional but it is an added advantage) 
- Two or three recommendation letter from a Professor, Associate Professor or any other lecturers that can write about your academic prowess. 
- International passport 
- Faith in Almighty God.

06/12/2022, 5:37â€¯pm - BoluğŸ‘©â€âš–ï¸: Slide 5

There are scholarships opportunities all over the world... You should decide with an informed mind...Not because your friends are going to the US, UK, Canada or this and that. Each country has requirements and discipline standards varies across the world.

Some US schools are leading in certain disciplines, same with the UK, Canada, Germany, France, Poland, New Zealand, Hong Kong, and other countries. Your decision should be based on your discipline ranking, University ranking, job prospect after graduation among other key factors to be considered. Also, you should apply for scholarships selectively, especially those with application fees. Don't waste money when you don't even meet the basic requirements...

Most scholarship applications are free* save for application fees,Â  don't pay agents to do the application for you...Well, if you have the cash to throw around, you can go ahead; and if you are not really after scholarships, you just want to leave the country.
06/12/2022, 5:37â€¯pm - BoluğŸ‘©â€âš–ï¸: Slide 6
How do you write the scholarship essay?

Usually a guide is usually provided in the scholarship application requirements. If they did, you should follow that. If they have not specified a specific format, then you can follow this simple outline when making your application/motivation letter: (1) Background/Key Qualifications, (2) Intentions for studying, (3) Expectations of the Course, and (4) your plans during and after the study. In making the letter, you should not just tell them why you need the scholarship but more importantly you shouldÂ  explain clearly why you deserve to get the scholarship.
You can get a sample of this online by just searching on Google.
06/12/2022, 5:37â€¯pm - BoluğŸ‘©â€âš–ï¸: Slide 7

Preparing to Write Scholarship Essays

I have a friend who writes his scholarship essays 6 months before the scholarship opening and share with people for proofreading and adjustment. 

Please write, proofread, Proofread again, proofread again before submitting your write ups for scholarships. I advise you shard with scholars in your field who have won scholarships in the past.
06/12/2022, 5:37â€¯pm - BoluğŸ‘©â€âš–ï¸: slide 8
Yes, there are scholarships for direct PhD without masters usually in the US.

Direct PhD is not meant for first class graduates only in the US...It is all about how you can package your applications. Your experience, volunteering, online and offline courses also counts. 

In essence, scholarship application is all about planning and knowing your onions. Failure to plan and package your application very well will likely lead to rejection irrespective of your grade.

Something like:

Dear XYZ

We received applications from many qualified candidates like you but unfortunately we have applicants with better...ğŸŒš

I must emphasise that rejection mails are part of scholarship applications...You win some, you lose some. Your rejection mail is a testimony that you have tried but there are some useless rejection mails as a result of your own doing. Don't just submit for submitting sake...Submit a good application.
I got many rejection before winning three scholarships. I got 23 rejections then. 

it's normal but that shouldn't stop you from applying again. Reevaluate yourself and retire again. Â Â 

I'm laying emphasis on this because it is a normal thing...and you shouldn't back out when you are at the receiving end. Just imagine receiving a rejection mail thru DHL.

"Well packaged and expensive rejection mail" (copied)

11/12/2022, 8:49â€¯pm - +234 816 537 7962: *Swift to hear, slow to speak, slow to anger*

I came home from work, tired. I sat down on the sofa and put my feet up. My wife brought me a glass of water. My son gave me a sheet of paper and I read through:

English              17%
Biology              35%
Mathematics   40%
Physics             37%
Chemistry         42%
Economics       12%
Agriculture.      19%
Geography        22%

Suddenly, I lost my temper and started shouting: "What is this? All the time you are on the phone and TV! How dare you bring me such marks? How dare you?"
My wife said: "Be patient. Listen...." But I interjected, "Shut up! It's your love and pampering that have spoilt him. He is no good and never serious at all!"
My Wife said: "Oh?"
I shouted: "No one in our family has performed so badly, ever!"
My son said: "Dad, I am sorry I made you angry. I was cleaning the old cupboard and I found this. It is your old school report card, dated 27th July 1977 sir." I looked at the top and it was my report sheet. My name was boldly inscribed on it! 
I became humbled, gentle, and dumbfounded. Imagine the atmosphere afterward. Calmness in the air. With a foolish grin on my face, I replied, "Son, you know, in those days, food was scarce."

*NYSC mobilization process â€“ Step by step*

Below are the process of NYSC mobilization exercise;

1. *Clearance in school:* NYSC mobilization starts right from this point. Graduates are expected to complete their final clearance in their respective institutions.

2. *Get your statement of results:* 
After completing your final clearance, next is to get your statement of results. Statement of results will be needed for registration in the NYSC Orientation Camp.

3. *Sign up for NYSC:* While waiting for your statement of result to be ready, you should proceed to register for NYSC at the Studentsâ€™ Affairs Directorate in your school.

4. *Verify your name on JAMB Matriculation list:* Itâ€™s important to verify your name on the JAMB matriculated list. If your name is not on this list, you will not be able to register for NYSC.

5. *Verify your name on the Senate list:* Your institution will upload names of those who are eligible to serve on the NYSC portal. After they have uploaded the list, proceed to verify your name.

6. *NYSC online registration:* Only those whose names are on the NYSC Senate list will be eligible to register for NYSC.

7. *Print NYSC Call up letter:* After NYSC online registration, next is to wait for NYSC call up letter to be out. This letter will show you the state NYSC deployed you, date to report and other vital information.

8. *Get the required documents:* Make sure all your documents are ready, because you need them in NYSC Orientation Camp for registration.


*ADMIN*

*NYSC mobilization process â€“ Step by step*

Below are the process of NYSC mobilization exercise;

1. *Clearance in school:* NYSC mobilization starts right from this point. Graduates are expected to complete their final clearance in their respective institutions.

2. *Get your statement of results:* 
After completing your final clearance, next is to get your statement of results. Statement of results will be needed for registration in the NYSC Orientation Camp.

3. *Sign up for NYSC:* While waiting for your statement of result to be ready, you should proceed to register for NYSC at the Studentsâ€™ Affairs Directorate in your school.

4. *Verify your name on JAMB Matriculation list:* Itâ€™s important to verify your name on the JAMB matriculated list. If your name is not on this list, you will not be able to register for NYSC.

5. *Verify your name on the Senate list:* Your institution will upload names of those who are eligible to serve on the NYSC portal. After they have uploaded the list, proceed to verify your name.

6. *NYSC online registration:* Only those whose names are on the NYSC Senate list will be eligible to register for NYSC.

7. *Print NYSC Call up letter:* After NYSC online registration, next is to wait for NYSC call up letter to be out. This letter will show you the state NYSC deployed you, date to report and other vital information.

8. *Get the required documents:* Make sure all your documents are ready, because you need them in NYSC Orientation Camp for registration.
